I've uploaded a code repository in the directory . Consider the following PR description:

<pr_description>
[BUG] Audio.equals() and Audio.hashCode() use Objects.equals on byte[] field, breaking content-based comparison
**Describe the bug**

The `Audio` class (`dev.langchain4j.data.audio.Audio`) uses `Objects.equals()` and `Objects.hash()` for its `byte[] binaryData` field. However, arrays in Java do not override `equals()` and `hashCode()` from `Object`, so these methods compare references instead of contents.

As a result, two `Audio` instances with identical binary content are incorrectly treated as different objects, which breaks usage in `Set<Audio>`, `Map<Audio, ?>`, `List.contains()`, and `List.remove()`.

Current implementation in `Audio.java`:

```java
@Override
public boolean equals(Object o) {
    if (this == o) return true;
    if (o == null || getClass() != o.getClass()) return false;
    Audio that = (Audio) o;
    return Objects.equals(this.url, that.url)
            && Objects.equals(this.binaryData, that.binaryData)  // ❌ compares references, not content
            && Objects.equals(this.base64Data, that.base64Data)
            && Objects.equals(this.mimeType, that.mimeType);
}

@Override
public int hashCode() {
    return Objects.hash(url, binaryData, base64Data, mimeType);  // ❌ uses identity hashCode for byte[]
}
```

**Log and Stack trace**

N/A — this is a logical bug, not a runtime exception. No stack trace is produced; the issue manifests as silently incorrect equality results.

**To Reproduce**

```java
byte[] data1 = {1, 2, 3};
byte[] data2 = {1, 2, 3};  // Identical content, different reference

Audio audio1 = Audio.builder().binaryData(data1).mimeType("audio/wav").build();
Audio audio2 = Audio.builder().binaryData(data2).mimeType("audio/wav").build();

// All of the following currently fail:
assertThat(audio1).isEqualTo(audio2);
assertThat(audio1.hashCode()).isEqualTo(audio2.hashCode());

Set<Audio> set = new HashSet<>();
set.add(audio1);
assertThat(set.contains(audio2)).isTrue();
```

**Expected behavior**

Two `Audio` instances with identical field values (including identical binary content) should be considered equal and produce the same hash code, in line with Java's `equals` / `hashCode` contract.

**Please complete the following information:**
- LangChain4j version: latest `main` branch (verified the bug still exists)
- LLM(s) used: N/A — this affects the core data class, independent of any model provider
- Java version: 21
- Spring Boot version (if applicable): N/A

**Additional context**

**Precedent in the codebase:** The `Embedding` class (`dev.langchain4j.data.embedding.Embedding`) in the same `langchain4j-core` module already correctly handles its `float[] vector` field using `Arrays.equals()` and `Arrays.hashCode()`. The fix for `Audio` should follow the same pattern.

**Other classes inspected:** I checked all media data classes in `dev.langchain4j.data.*`:

| Class | Has `byte[]` field? | Status |
|-------|---------------------|--------|
| `Audio` | ✅ `byte[] binaryData` | ❌ **Has bug** |
| `Image` | ❌ only `String base64Data` | ✅ OK |
| `Video` | ❌ only `String base64Data` | ✅ OK |
| `PdfFile` | ❌ only `String base64Data` | ✅ OK |

`Audio` is the only class affected — this is an isolated issue, likely introduced when `binaryData` was added as a second representation alongside `base64Data` to support implementations like Azure OpenAI that require raw binary audio data.

**Backward compatibility note:** This is technically a behavioral change (some `equals()` calls that previously returned `false` will now return `true`), but the previous behavior violates Java's `equals` contract and no reasonable code should depend on it. The fix aligns with the existing correct pattern in `Embedding`.

**Willing to submit a PR:** I'd be happy to submit a draft PR for this fix following the pattern from `Embedding`, if you'd like me to proceed.

</pr_description>

    98	                && Objects.equals(this.base64Data, that.base64Data)
    99	                && Objects.equals(this.mimeType, that.mimeType);
   100	    }
   101	
   102	    @Override
   103	    public int hashCode() {
   104	        return Objects.hash(url, binaryData, base64Data, mimeType);
   105	    }
   106	
   107	    @Override
   108	    public String toString() {
   109	        return "Audio {" + " url = "
   110	                + quoted(url) + ", base64Data = "
   111	                + quoted(base64Data) + ", mimeType = "
   112	                + quoted(mimeType) + " }";
   113	    }
   114	
   115	    /**
   116	     * Builder for {@link Audio}.
   117	     */
   118	    public static class Builder {
   119	
   120	        private URI url;
   121	        private byte[] binaryData;
   122	        private String base64Data;
   123	        private String mimeType;
   124	
   125	        /**
   126	         * Create a new {@link Builder}.
   127	         */
   128	        public Builder() {}
   129	
   130	        /**
   131	         * Set the url of the audio.
   132	         *
   133	         * @param url the url of the audio.
   134	         * @return {@code this}
   135	         */
   136	        public Builder url(URI url) {
   137	            this.url = url;
   138	            return this;
   139	        }
   140	
   141	        /**
   142	         * Set the url of the audio.
   143	         *
   144	         * @param url the url of the audio.
   145	         * @return {@code this}
   146	         */
   147	        public Builder url(String url) {
   148	            return url(URI.create(url));
   149	        }
   150	
   151	        /**
   152	         * Set the raw binary data of the audio as a byte array.
   153	         * This is the preferred format for implementations like Azure OpenAI that require
   154	         * raw binary audio data for processing.
   155	         *
   156	         * @param binaryData the raw binary data of the audio as a byte array.
   157	         * @return {@code this}
   158	         */
   159	        public Builder binaryData(byte[] binaryData) {
   160	            this.binaryData = binaryData;
   161	            return this;
   162	        }
   163	
   164	        /**
   165	         * Set the Base64 encoded string representation of the audio data.
   166	         * This is the preferred format for implementations like OpenAI that accept
   167	         * Base64 encoded audio data in API requests.
   168	         *
   169	         * @param base64Data the Base64 encoded string representation of the audio.
   170	         * @return {@code this}
   171	         */
   172	        public Builder base64Data(String base64Data) {
   173	            this.base64Data = base64Data;
   174	            return this;
   175	        }
   176	
   177	        /**
   178	         * Set the mime type of the audio.
   179	         *
   180	         * @param mimeType the mime type of the audio.
   181	         * @return {@code this}
   182	         */
   183	        public Builder mimeType(String mimeType) {
   184	            this.mimeType = mimeType;
   185	            return this;
   186	        }
   187	
   188	        /**
   189	         * Build the {@link Audio}.
   190	         *
   191	         * @return the {@link Audio}.
   192	         */
   193	        public Audio build() {
   194	            return new Audio(this);

     1	package dev.langchain4j.data.embedding;
     2	
     3	import java.util.ArrayList;
     4	import java.util.Arrays;
     5	import java.util.List;
     6	
     7	import static dev.langchain4j.internal.ValidationUtils.ensureNotNull;
     8	
     9	/**
    10	 * Represents a dense vector embedding of a text.
    11	 * This class encapsulates a float array that captures the "meaning" or semantic information of the text.
    12	 * Texts with similar meanings will have their vectors located close to each other in the embedding space.
    13	 * The embeddings are typically created by embedding models.
    14	 * @see dev.langchain4j.model.embedding.EmbeddingModel
    15	 */
    16	public class Embedding {
    17	
    18	    private final float[] vector;
    19	
    20	    /**
    21	     * Creates a new Embedding.
    22	     * @param vector the vector, takes ownership of the array.
    23	     */
    24	    public Embedding(float[] vector) {
    25	        this.vector = ensureNotNull(vector, "vector");
    26	    }
    27	
    28	    /**
    29	     * Returns the vector.
    30	     * @return the vector.
    31	     */
    32	    public float[] vector() {
    33	        return vector;
    34	    }
    35	
    36	    /**
    37	     * Returns a copy of the vector as a list.
    38	     * @return the vector as a list.
    39	     */
    40	    public List<Float> vectorAsList() {
    41	        List<Float> list = new ArrayList<>(vector.length);
    42	        for (float f : vector) {
    43	            list.add(f);
    44	        }
    45	        return list;
    46	    }
    47	
    48	    /**
    49	     * Normalize vector
    50	     */
    51	    public void normalize() {
    52	        double norm = 0.0;
    53	        for (float f : vector) {
    54	            norm += f * f;
    55	        }
    56	        norm = Math.sqrt(norm);
    57	        if (Math.abs(norm) < 1e-10) {
    58	            return;
    59	        }
    60	        for (int i = 0; i < vector.length; i++) {
    61	            vector[i] /= (float) norm;
    62	        }
    63	    }
    64	
    65	    /**
    66	     * Returns the dimension of the vector.
    67	     * @return the dimension of the vector.
    68	     */
    69	    public int dimension() {
    70	        return vector.length;
    71	    }
    72	
    73	    @Override
    74	    public boolean equals(Object o) {
    75	        if (this == o) return true;
    76	        if (o == null || getClass() != o.getClass()) return false;
    77	        Embedding that = (Embedding) o;
    78	        return Arrays.equals(this.vector, that.vector);
    79	    }
    80	
    81	    @Override
    82	    public int hashCode() {
    83	        return Arrays.hashCode(vector);
    84	    }
    85	
    86	    @Override
    87	    public String toString() {
    88	        return "Embedding {" +
    89	                " vector = " + Arrays.toString(vector) +
    90	                " }";
    91	    }
    92	
    93	    /**
    94	     * Creates a new Embedding from the given vector.
    95	     * @param vector the vector, takes ownership of the array.
    96	     * @return the new Embedding.
    97	     */
    98	    public static Embedding from(float[] vector) {
    99	        return new Embedding(vector);
   100	    }
   101	
   102	    /**
   103	     * Creates a new Embedding from the given vector.
   104	     * @param vector the vector.
   105	     * @return the new Embedding.
   106	     */
   107	    public static Embedding from(List<Float> vector) {
   108	        float[] array = new float[vector.size()];
   109	        for (int i = 0; i < vector.size(); i++) {
   110	            array[i] = vector.get(i);
   111	        }
   112	        return new Embedding(array);
   113	    }
   114	}

🎬 ACTION
cd /testbed && cat > /tmp/ReproduceBug.java << 'EOF'
import dev.langchain4j.data.audio.Audio;
import java.util.HashSet;
import java.util.Set;

public class ReproduceBug {
    public static void main(String[] args) {
        byte[] data1 = {1, 2, 3};
        byte[] data2 = {1, 2, 3};  // Identical content, different reference

        Audio audio1 = Audio.builder().binaryData(data1).mimeType("audio/wav").build();
        Audio audio2 = Audio.builder().binaryData(data2).mimeType("audio/wav").build();

        System.out.println("audio1.equals(audio2): " + audio1.equals(audio2) + " (expected: true)");
        System.out.println("audio1.hashCode() == audio2.hashCode(): " + (audio1.hashCode() == audio2.hashCode()) + " (expected: true)");

        Set<Audio> set = new HashSet<>();
        set.add(audio1);
        System.out.println("set.contains(audio2): " + set.contains(audio2) + " (expected: true)");

        // Check if any assertion failed
        boolean failed = false;
        if (!audio1.equals(audio2)) {
            System.out.println("FAIL: equals() returned false for identical content!");
            failed = true;
        }
        if (audio1.hashCode() != audio2.hashCode()) {
            System.out.println("FAIL: hashCode() differs for identical content!");
            failed = true;
        }
        if (!set.contains(audio2)) {
            System.out.println("FAIL: HashSet.contains() failed for identical content!");
            failed = true;
        }
        if (failed) {
            System.exit(1);
        } else {
            System.out.println("All checks passed!");
        }
    }
}
EOF

    11	 * This class supports multiple formats for storing audio:
    12	 *
